				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Oster-Oratorium, BWV 249 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>11 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725, revised ca.1738, ca.1743/1746, 1749
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_oratorios&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred oratorios</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Oratorios&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Oratorios</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="33 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_4_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 4 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <td>BWV 249&#160;; BC D 8a I-II; BC D 8b I-II
</td></tr>

<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 457
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>11 movements:
<ol><li> Sinfonia
</li><li> Adagio
</li><li> Duetto e Coro: Kommt, eilet und laufet; Duetto: Komm, gehet und eilet (1st-2nd versions)
</li><li> Recitativo (SATB): O kalter Männer Sinn!
</li><li> Aria (Soprano): Seele, deine Spezereien
</li><li> Recitativo (ATB): Hier ist die Gruft
</li><li> Aria (Tenor): Sanfte soll mein Todeskummer
</li><li> Recitativo (SA): Indessen seufzen wir
</li><li> Aria (Alto): Saget, saget mir geschwinde
</li><li> Recitativo (Bass): Wir sind erfreut
</li><li> Chorus: Preis und Dank
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

</th></tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="33%" style="background-color:rgb(241,220,143)">
<ul><li>BWV 244 <i><a href="/wiki/Matth%C3%A4uspassion,_BWV_244_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Matthäuspassion, BWV 244 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Matthäuspassion</a></i>
</li><li>BWV 244a <i>Klagt, Kinder, klagt es aller Welt</i>
</li><li>BWV 245 <i><a href="/wiki/Johannespassion,_BWV_245_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Johannespassion, BWV 245 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Johannespassion</a></i>
</li><li>BWV 246 <i><a href="/wiki/Lukaspassion,_BWV_246_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Lukaspassion, BWV 246 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Lukaspassion</a></i>
</li><li>BWV 247 <i>Markuspassion</i>
</li></ul>
</td>
<td valign="top" width="33%" style="background-color:rgb(241,220,143)">
<ul><li>BWV 248 <i><a href="/wiki/Weihnachts-Oratorium,_BWV_248_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Weihnachts-Oratorium, BWV 248 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Weihnachts-Oratorium</a></i> (Psalm 117)
</li><li>BWV 249 <i>Cantata</i>
</li><li>BWV 249/1 <i>Kommt, eilet und laufet</i>
</li><li>BWV 249/2 <i><strong class="selflink">Oster-Oratorium</strong></i>
</li><li>BWV 249a <i>Entfliehet, verschwindet, entweichet, ihr Sorgen</i>
</li><li>BWV 249b <i>Verjaget, zerstreuet, zerrütet, ihr Sterne</i>
</li></ul>
</td></tr>
</table>
